)@@G@@QF000*  .   @[@@@@.     @D@@@@. SINGLE-FILE MODE WAS SPECIFIED, SO WE'LLHT
)@@G@@ GET THE    @E@@@@. INFORMATION ABOUT A PARTICULAR FILE WITHOUT DOING A HU
)@@G@@DGET$.@[@@@@.     @E@@@@. 1. FIRST, ATTACH AN INTERNAL NAME TO THE SPECIHV
)@@G@@FIED FILE.  @F@@@@. 2. NOW TRY AN ER FITEM$ ON THAT FILE.  IF IT DOES NOHW

)@@G@@EM$ DOES WORK,    @B@@@@.    THE FILE IS ASSIGNED BY THE USER.    @F@@@@HY

)@@G@@@ @@@@.    THEN GO ON TO STEP 5.    @F@@@@. 4. FILE IS CATALOGUED MASS SIE
)@@G@@TORAGE OR TAPE FILE, AND MAY OR MAY @F@@@@.    NOT BE ASSIGNED BY THE USIF
)@@G@@ER.  AN ER MSCON$ IS NOW DONE, USING@G@@@@.    THE DREAD$ FUNCTION, TO OIG
)@@G@@BTAIN THE DIRECTORY INFORMATION FOR THIS  @F@@@@.    FILE.  FIRST THE LEIH
)@@G@@AD ITEM IS READ, AND THEN THE MAIN ITEM.  @G@@@@.    CHECKS ARE MADE TO II
)@@G@@DETERMINE WHETHER THE FILE IS REMOVABLE DISC,   @D@@@@.    TAPE, OR G-OPIJ
)@@G@@TION, AND APPROPRIATE FLAGS ARE SET.@G@@@@. 5. IF THE FILE IS NOT ASSIGNIK
)@@G@@ED BY THE USER, OR IF IT IS A TAPE FILE,  @H@@@@.    THIS STEP IS SKIPPEIL
)@@G@@D.  IF NOT, WE LOAD THE RUN'S PCT BANK, VIA AN LDJ    @H@@@@.    (OR ER IM
)@@G@@PCT$), AND FIND THE FILE DESCRIPTION ENTRY FOR THIS FILE.  THIS   @F@@@@IN
)@@G@@.    IS THE ONLY WAY TO FIND THE GRANULE COUNTS AND PACKIDS FOR   @G@@@@IO
)@@G@@.    TEMPORARY FIXED AND REMOVABLE MASS STORAGE FILES, AND SOMETIMES    IP

)@@G@@@G@@@@.    AS WELL.  AFTER GATHERING AS MUCH INFORMATION AS IS USEFUL FOIR

)@@G@@.    FOR TEMPORARY REMOVABLE DISC FILES, ADDITIONAL CODE IS NEEDED TO   IT
)@@G@@@G@@@@.    OBTAIN A COPY OF THE FASTRAND-FORMAT MASS STORAGE AVAILABILTYIU

)@@G@@@G@@@@. CONTINUATION OF 'PCTDAD' SUBROUTINE.  FINDS NEXT DAD/GRANULE ITEYB
)@@G@@M     @E@@@@. (FOR A PARTICULAR FILE) IN THE PCT, AND RETURNS IT TO THE YC

)@@G@@MJ A3,PCTLNK  OBTAIN CORRECT PCT BLOCK    @E@@@@          SA,H1     A0,PYJ
)@@G@@CTDADN        STORE ADDR OF NEW ITEM@E@@@@          LA,H2     A1,0,A0   YK
)@@G@@        GET LINK TO NEXT ITEM @F@@@@          SA,H2     A1,PCTDADN      YL

)@@G@@        ERRPR$            EDIT THE INFO (IF ERRPR$ IS UNDEFINED,  @I@@@@AZ

)@@G@@**(LDJOK=0) @[@@@@.     @F@@@@. THIS SUBROUTINE IS FOR USE WHEN LDJ OF PCB
)@@G@@CT BANK IS NOT DESIRED  @F@@@@. (LDJOK EQU 0).  IT CONVERTS THE RELATVIECC
)@@G@@ PCT BUFFER ADDRESS     @G@@@@. INTO AN ADDRESS USABLE BY  ER PCT$, AND CD
)@@G@@LOADS THE PROPER PCT BLOCK.   @G@@@@. UPON EXIT, A0 CONTAINS THE ADDRESSCE
)@@G@@ WITHIN PCTBUF CORRESPONDING TO     @A@@@@. THE DESIRED PCT RELATIVE ADDCF
)@@G@@RESS. @[@@@@.     @H@@@@PCTLNK    TG,U      A0,PCTBUF+01000   ADDR IN CUCG
)@@G@@RRENTLY-LOADED PCT BLOCK?     @B@@@@          J         NOTCUR          CH
)@@G@@  NO  @E@@@@          L         A1,A0             YES, GET ADDR IN A1   CI
)@@G@@@H@@@@          AN        A1,X4             SUBTRACT REL PCTBUF ADDR, LECJ
)@@G@@AVING LINK  @F@@@@          A         A1,PCTNAM         ADD CURRENT ITEMCK
)@@G@@ BASE ADDR  @E@@@@          S         A1,PCTNAM         STORE NEW BASE ACL
)@@G@@DDR   @H@@@@          J         0,A3              RETURN WITH A0=REL ADDCM
)@@G@@R WITHIN PCTBUF   @[@@@@.     @ @@@@. DESIRED BLOCK NOT IN PCTBUF @[@@@@CN
)@@G@@.     @H@@@@NOTCUR    AN        A0,X4             SUBTRACT REL PCTBUF ADCO
)@@G@@DR, LEAVING LINK  @E@@@@          A,H2      A0,PCTNAM         ADD CURRENCP
)@@G@@T ITEM BASE @D@@@@          S,H2      A0,PCTNAM         STORE NEW BASE  CQ
)@@G@@@E@@@@          AND,U     A0,0777000        ISOLATE BLOCK NUMBER  @D@@@@CR
)@@G@@          A,U       A1,01000          ADJUST FOR PCT$ @D@@@@          LXCS
)@@G@@I,U     A1,01000          GET 1 PCT BLOCK @D@@@@          S         A0,ACT
)@@G@@2             SAVE REL ADDR   @E@@@@          L,U       A0,PCTBUF       CU
)@@G@@  GET ADDR OF PCT BUFFER@D@@@@          ER        PCT$              GET CV
)@@G@@PCT BLOCK   @D@@@@          L         A0,A2             RETRIEVE ADDR   CW
)@@G@@@E@@@@          AND,U     A0,0777           MASK OUT BLOCK INFO   @F@@@@CX
)@@G@@          L,U       A0,PCTBUF,A1      FORM REL ADDR INTO PCTBUF   @C@@@@CY
)@@G@@          J         0,A3              RETURN    @B@@@@          OFF     CZ
)@@G@@  (CHKPCT>0)**(LDJOK=0) @F@@@@/. CSF$ CONTINGENCY ROUTINE FOR BAD FILENADA
)@@G@@ME INPUT VIA READ$.     @[@@@@.     @^@@@@QF700     +         0D  @F@@@@DB
)@@G@@          LA,T1     A0,QF700          GET ERROR TYPE AND CODE     @F@@@@DC

)@@G@@        QF900             AND TRY ANOTHER DATA CARD   @E@@@@QF710     TEDG
)@@G@@,U      A0,0401           ER INDEX OUT OF RANGE?@E@@@@          TNE,U   DH

)@@G@@              YES, MAY BE ATTEMPT AT ER ERRPR$  @F@@@@          ER      DJ

)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @G@@@@QF900*    SR        R15,SFMODE        RESET SINGLE-FILDP

)@@G@@ SORT INTERFACE ROUTINES@[@@@@.     @[@@@@.     @G@@@@. M.I. SEC 0 WORDSEC
)@@G@@ 18-19, WHICH CONTAIN THE DATE/TIME OF LAST REFERENCE @G@@@@. AND OF CATED
)@@G@@ALOGUING, ARE MODIFIED SO THAT THEY ARE MORE EASILY SORTED. @[@@@@.     EE
)@@G@@@H@@@@.     ------------------------------------------------------------EF

)@@G@@TIME              :     @H@@@@.     ------------------------------------EH
)@@G@@-------------------------------     @B@@@@.     :                       EI

)@@G@@, ETC.@[@@@@.     @H@@@@.     ------------------------------------------EL

)@@G@@@ @@@@. IN A15 BY 'CHECK' ROUTINE.  @[@@@@.     @^@@@@          AXR$    ET

)@@G@@  GRAND TOTALS?   @B@@@@          J         TOT090            YES @C@@@@IC
)@@G@@          E$DIT     EDPACK            OPEN EDIT @D@@@@          E$MSG   ID
)@@G@@  TOTALS            START MESSAGE   @D@@@@          LA        A0,BRKCNT IE
)@@G@@        GET BREAK COUNT @G@@@@          ANA       A0,X4             NUMBIF
)@@G@@ER OF LOWER LEVELS TO SKIP    @G@@@@          MSI,H1    A0,BRKPNT       IG
)@@G@@  MULTIPLY BY LENGTH OF ENTRIES     @E@@@@          LX        X5,BRKPNT IH
)@@G@@        GET TABLE POINTER     @G@@@@          AX        X5,A0           II
)@@G@@  SKIP PROPER NUMBER OF ENTRIES     @G@@@@          LR        R4,X4     IJ
)@@G@@        MOVE CURRENT BREAK LEVEL TO R4    @E@@@@          JGD       R4,$IK
)@@G@@+1            ADJUST FOR LOOP COUNT @F@@@@TOT020    LA,H2     A0,BRKSPECIL
)@@G@@,X5     GET 1ST 3 CHARS OF SPEC     @H@@@@          LX        X10,(3,TOTIM
)@@G@@TAB-3)  INITIALIZE SEARCH INDEX AND INCREMENT   @E@@@@          LR,U    IN
)@@G@@  R1,TOTTABL        SET SEARCH LENGTH     @E@@@@          SE,H1     A0,3IO
)@@G@@,*X10         FIND SPEC IN TABLE?   @C@@@@          J         TOTWHAT   IP
)@@G@@        NO, USE ??@G@@@@          LA        A0,BRKVAL,X5      LOAD FORMEIQ
)@@G@@R CONTENTS OF FIELD     @F@@@@          EX        2,X10             YES,IR
)@@G@@ JUMP TO PROPER ROUTINE @]@@@@TOTWHAT   . @G@@@@          TP        BRKLIS
)@@G@@OAD,X5        IS VALUE TWO FIELDATA WORDS (DL ?)@D@@@@          J       IT
)@@G@@  TOTWHAT3          YES, HANDLE IT  @B@@@@          E$FD1     ('SPEC  ')IU

)@@G@@@C@@@@          E$COPY    3,(' =    ')      SPACE OVER@G@@@@          DLIW
)@@G@@        A0,BRKVAL,X5      PICK UP VALUE AND MASK (IF ANY)   @D@@@@      IX

)@@G@@  A0,A1             MASK OFF PROPER BIT   @E@@@@          LA,U      A0,0IZ

)@@G@@        TOT060            GO ON TO NEXT LEVEL   @D@@@@TOTWHAT3  LX,U    JD

)@@G@@        WE DON'T KNOW WHAT IT IS, BUT PRINT IT  @]@@@@TOTFD2    . @E@@@@JF
)@@G@@          E$FD2     0,X10             EDIT KEY FIELD NAME   @C@@@@      JG
)@@G@@    E$SKIP    1                 SPACE OVER@E@@@@          E$FD2     BRKVJH

)@@G@@LUE   @A@@@@          TE        A0,('      ')   @D@@@@          TNZ     JM

)@@G@@@]@@@@TOT050    . @E@@@@          E$FD2     0,X10             EDIT TYPE KT
)@@G@@OF FILE     @]@@@@TOT060    . @E@@@@          E$CHAR    ','             KU

)@@G@@ SDF OUTPUT ROUTINE     @[@@@@.     @F@@@@. CALLED IF W-OPTION IS SET.  OP
)@@G@@WRITES EACH QUALIFIER*FILENAME(CYC) @F@@@@. INTO SDF FILE WHOSE NAME IS OQ

)@@G@@@C@@@@. SDF INITIALIZATION:  SET UP FCT AND OPEN SDFO @[@@@@.     @E@@@@PE

)@@G@@*[S@@@*SDFF*@F@@@@. @MFD SNAP$ ROUTINE - DUMPS DIRECTORY ITEMS SELECTED SL
)@@G@@BY THE USER @[@@@@.     @^@@@@          AXR$      .   @G@@@@          COSM
)@@G@@NFIG    .                 DEFINE CONFIGURATION PARAMTERES   @ @@@@      SN
)@@G@@    ON        SNAPOK    @D@@@@          EQUFS     .                 DEFISO
)@@G@@NE TAGS     @D@@@@PRT       FORM      12,6,18           FORM T1,S3,H2   SP
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @^@@@@P         PROC      1   @^@@@@SNAPP*    NAME      0   SQ
)@@G@@@^@@@@SETSNAP*  NAME      1   @F@@@@          DO P(1)=0 , GO ERONLY     SR
)@@G@@  SKIP IF NO PARAMETERS GIVEN @D@@@@          LA        A0,(P(1,1))     SS
)@@G@@  GET HEADER INFO @H@@@@          DO OLDMFD=0 , GO ON         SKIP 'DAD'ST
)@@G@@ CHECK IF NEW FORMAT ONLY     @E@@@@       DO 1-(P(1,1)='DAD   ') , GO OSU
)@@G@@N SKIP IF NOT 'DAD'     @E@@@@          TNZ       MFD$F             NEW SV
)@@G@@FORMAT DIRECTORY? @G@@@@          LA        A0,('GTB   ')     NO, USE 'GSW
)@@G@@TB' RATHER THAN 'DAD'   @^@@@@ON        NAME      .   @E@@@@          SASX
)@@G@@        A0,SNAPKT         STORE IN SNAP$ PACKET @E@@@@          LA,U    SY
)@@G@@  A0,P(1,2)         GET BUFFER ADDRESS    @F@@@@          SA        A0,BSZ
)@@G@@UFAD          STORE IT IN SNAP$ PACKET    @H@@@@          DO P(1)<3 , GOTA
)@@G@@ ERONLY       IF NOT SPECIFIED, LEAVE # WORDS AS IS   @F@@@@          LATB
)@@G@@,U      A0,P(1,3)         BUT IF SPECIFIED, USE IT    @E@@@@          SATC
)@@G@@        A0,NWRDS          SET # OF WORDS TO SNAP@^@@@@ERONLY    NAME    TD
)@@G@@  .   @G@@@@          DO P(0,0)>0 , GO AWAY       SKIP IF JUST SETTING UTE
)@@G@@P PACKET    @ @@@@          ON        SNAPSUB=0 @F@@@@          LA,U    TF
)@@G@@  A0,SNAPKT         GET SNAP$ PACKET ADDRESS    @D@@@@          ER      TG
)@@G@@  SNAP$             DO THE SNAP$    @ @@@@          OFF       SNAPSUB=0 TH
)@@G@@@ @@@@          ON        SNAPSUB   @D@@@@          LMJ       X10,SNAP$ TI
)@@G@@        DO THE SNAP$    @D@@@@          LA        A2,SNAP           RELOTJ
)@@G@@AD SNAP BITS@ @@@@          OFF       SNAPSUB   @G@@@@          SR      TK
)@@G@@  R15,SNAPKT+2      SET SNAPPED-SOMETHING INDICATOR   @C@@@@          DOTL
)@@G@@ (P(1,1)='LI0')++(P(1,1)='LI1') , ; @F@@@@          SR        R15,LISNPDTM
)@@G@@        SET LEAD-ITEM-SNAPPED FLAG  @^@@@@AWAY      NAME      .   @#@@@@TN
)@@G@@          END     @[@@@@.     @D@@@@SNAPKT    'SEC   '                  TO
)@@G@@  SNAP$ PACKET    @D@@@@          +         28,0              ASSUME 1 STP
)@@G@@ECTOR @^@@@@          +         0   @E@@@@NWRDS     EQUF      SNAPKT+1,,TQ
)@@G@@H1      # OF WORDS TO SNAP    @F@@@@BUFAD     EQUF      SNAPKT+1,,H2    TR
)@@G@@  ADDRESS OF BUFFER TO SNAP   @[@@@@.     @ @@@@          ON        CHKPTS
)@@G@@CT=0  @C@@@@TEMPGT    'TEMP FILE DAD SNAP NOT CONFIGURED'   @B@@@@TEMPGTTT
)@@G@@P   +         0200+($-TEMPGT),TEMPGT@ @@@@          OFF       CHKPCT=0  TU
)@@G@@@ @@@@          ON        CHKPCT    @E@@@@TDAD      ' SNAP OF DAD ITEMS TV
)@@G@@CURRENTLY IN PCT FOLLOWS'     @B@@@@TDADP     +         0200+($-TDAD),TDTW
)@@G@@AD    @ @@@@          ON        OLDMFD    @D@@@@TGTBF     'FIRST GRANULETX
)@@G@@ IN THIS GRANULE ITEM: &'     @ @@@@          OFF       OLDMFD    @ @@@@TY
)@@G@@          OFF       CHKPCT    @]@@@@$(1)      . @H@@@@/. PRINT ROUTINE ETZ
)@@G@@NTERS HERE WITH A2 = SNAP FLAG IF SNAP FLAG IS NONZERO.     @[@@@@.     UA
)@@G@@@F@@@@SN000*    SZ        SNAPKT+2          CLEAR SNAPPED-SOMETHING FLAGUB
)@@G@@@E@@@@          TZ        LISNPD            CAN WE SNAP LEAD ITEM?@D@@@@UC

)@@G@@ROUTINE     @ @@@@/         ON        POLDBG    @[@@@@.     @#@@@@. DEBUZA
)@@G@@G SNAPS     @[@@@@.     @G@@@@POLDBM    'TESTS = &   AOX = &   POLNTH = ZB
)@@G@@&   SORT = &   BRKCNT = &'    @F@@@@SSIZE     EQU       6               ZC
)@@G@@  SUPER SPEC TABLE ENTRY SIZE @E@@@@BRKSIZ    EQU       6               ZD
)@@G@@  BRKTBL ENTRY SIZE     @[@@@@.     @]@@@@SN900*    . @C@@@@          E$ZE
)@@G@@DIT     EDPACK            OPEN EDIT @C@@@@          E$MSG     POLDBM    ZF
)@@G@@        START MSG @ @@@@          E$DECV    TESTS     @^@@@@          E$ZG
)@@G@@MSGR    .   @^@@@@          E$OCTV    AOX @^@@@@          E$MSGR    .   ZH
)@@G@@@ @@@@          E$DECV    POLNTH    @#@@@@          E$MSGR  @^@@@@      ZI
)@@G@@    E$DECV    SORT@^@@@@          E$MSGR    .   @ @@@@          E$DECV  ZJ
)@@G@@  BRKCNT    @ @@@@          P$RINT    POUT2     @C@@@@          SNAPP   ZK
)@@G@@  'SSTAB ',SSTAB,SSIZE*NSSP   @B@@@@          SNAPP     'POLISH',POLISH,ZL
)@@G@@NSSP  @ @@@@          ON        BRKOK     @ @@@@          TNZ       BRKCZM
)@@G@@NT    @ @@@@          J         NOBREAK   @D@@@@          SNAPP     'BRKZN
)@@G@@TBL',BRKTBL,BRKMAX*BRKSIZ     @B@@@@          SNAPP     'BRKPNT',BRKPNT,ZO
)@@G@@1     @B@@@@          SNAPP     'INVALU',INVALU,1     @]@@@@NOBREAK   . ZP
)@@G@@@ @@@@          OFF       BRKOK     @D@@@@          P$RINT    ( PRT 1,0,ZQ
)@@G@@0)      SKIP A LINE     @G@@@@          L$OAD     INSEG,IN2020,1    RETUZR
)@@G@@RN TO INITIALIZATION SEGMENT  @ @@@@          OFF       POLDBG    @ @@@@ZS
)@@G@@/         ON        SNAPSUB   @[@@@@.     @F@@@@. THIS SUBROUTINE PEFORMZT
)@@G@@S A MORE READABLE SNAP$-TYPE DUMP THAN IS @G@@@@. AVAILABLE THROUGH ER SZU
)@@G@@NAP$.  IT INCLUDES A SHORTER FORMAT FOR DEMAND  @H@@@@. USE.  THIS ROUTIZV
)@@G@@NE IS USED ONLY IF CONFIG PARAMETER 'SNAPSUB' IS NONZERO.   @[@@@@.     ZW
)@@G@@@A@@@@.    ENTER VIA:  LMJ  X10,SNAP$     @G@@@@.     DESTROYS:  X4, X10ZX
)@@G@@, X11, A6, R2, R4, PLUS REGISTERS USED BY EDIT$ @[@@@@.     @]@@@@$(0)  ZY
)@@G@@    . @ @@@@ENTIRE    'ALL & WORDS = &'   @G@@@@LASTWD    RES       1   ZZ
)@@G@@              LAST WORD OF EACH LINE IS STORED  @E@@@@.                 AA
)@@G@@                    HERE FOR COMPARISON   @E@@@@WPL       RES       1   AB
)@@G@@              # OF WORDS PER LINE   @[@@@@.     @F@@@@SLEN      EQU     AC
)@@G@@  5                 WORDS/LINE FOR SHORT LISTING@F@@@@LLEN      EQU     AD
)@@G@@  8                 WORDS/LINE FOR LONG LISTING @[@@@@.     @]@@@@$(1),SAE
)@@G@@NAP$. @E@@@@          P$RINT    ( PRT 2,1,SNAPKT) PRINT SNAP HEADER     AF
)@@G@@@F@@@@          LA        A0,NWRDS          GET NUMBER OF WORDS TO SNAP AG
)@@G@@@F@@@@          AND,U     A0,077777         MASK OF XAR BITS TO BE SAFE AH
)@@G@@@F@@@@          JZ        A1,,X10           IF NO WORDS TO SNAP, RETURN AI
)@@G@@@G@@@@          SA        A1,NWRDS          OTHERWISE, PUT MASKED # WORDAJ
)@@G@@S BACK@E@@@@          LX        X4,(1,0)          INITIALIZE WORD INDEX AK
)@@G@@@E@@@@          AX        X4,BUFAD          ADD BUFFER ADDRESS    @G@@@@AL
)@@G@@          TLE,U     A1,4              IF ONLY 1-3 WORDS BEING SNAPPED,  AM
)@@G@@@F@@@@          J         NOTSAM               SKIP ALL-THE-SAME TEST   AN
)@@G@@@F@@@@          AN,U      A1,1              MINUS 1 FOR SEARCH COUNT    AO
)@@G@@@D@@@@          SA        A1,R1             SET SEARCH COUNT@H@@@@      AP
)@@G@@    LX        A2,X4             COPY WORD INDEX AND INCREMENT TO A2     AQ
)@@G@@@E@@@@          LA        A0,0,A2           GET 1ST WORD OF AREA  @F@@@@AR
)@@G@@          SNE       A0,1,*A2          FIND ANY DIFFERENT WORDS?   @D@@@@AS
)@@G@@          J         $+2               NO, ALL THE SAME@E@@@@          J AT
)@@G@@        NOTSAM            YES, NOT ALL THE SAME @[@@@@.     @D@@@@. THE AU
)@@G@@ENTIRE AREA IS EQUAL:  PRINT MESSAGE AND RETURN @[@@@@.     @C@@@@      AV
)@@G@@    E$DIT     EDPACK            OPEN EDIT @C@@@@          E$MSG     ENTIAW
)@@G@@RE            START MSG @E@@@@          E$DECV    NWRDS             EDITAX
)@@G@@ NUMBER OF WORDS  @D@@@@          E$MSGR    .                 CONTINUE MAY
)@@G@@SG    @C@@@@          E$OCTV    0,X4              ADD VALUE @C@@@@      AZ
)@@G@@    P$RINT    POUT              PRINT MSG @C@@@@          J         0,X1BA
)@@G@@0             RETURN    @[@@@@.     @D@@@@. ENTIRE AREA IS NOT EQUAL:  DBB
)@@G@@UMP IT LINE BY LINE     @[@@@@.     @E@@@@NOTSAM    LA        A0,( PRT 1BC
)@@G@@,0,0)   GET SET TO SKIP A LINE@D@@@@          TZ        LONGLIST        BD
)@@G@@  LONG LISTING?   @C@@@@          ER        PRINT$            YES, DO ITBE
)@@G@@@E@@@@          LA        A0,NWRDS          GET # OF WORDS TO SNAP@E@@@@BF
)@@G@@          DSL       A0,36             GET SET FOR DIVIDE    @E@@@@      BG
)@@G@@    LA,U      A2,SLEN           GET SHORT WORDS/LINE  @D@@@@          TZBH
)@@G@@        LONGLIST          LONG LISTING?   @F@@@@          LA,U      A2,LBI
)@@G@@LEN           YES, GET LONG WORDS/LINE    @E@@@@          SA        A2,WBJ
)@@G@@PL            STORE WORDS PER LINE  @F@@@@          DI        A0,A2     BK
)@@G@@        CALCULATE # OF LINES NEEDED @F@@@@          TZ        A1        BL
)@@G@@        REMAINDER ON PARTIAL LINE?  @B@@@@          AA,U      A0,1      BM
)@@G@@        YES @D@@@@          ANA,U     A0,1              ADJUST FOR JGD  BN
)@@G@@@D@@@@          SA        A0,R4             SET LOOP COUNT  @F@@@@      BO
)@@G@@    LA,U      A6,0              INITIALIZE SKIP INDICATOR   @F@@@@      BP
)@@G@@    J         PRINTLINE         ALWAYS PRINT FIRST LINE     @[@@@@.     BQ
)@@G@@@H@@@@. BEFORE PRINTING EACH LINE (EXCEPT THE FIRST AND LAST LINES), CHEBR
)@@G@@CK TO SEE   @H@@@@. IF ALL WORDS ON THIS LINE ARE EQUAL TO THE LAST WORDBS
)@@G@@ OF THE PREVIOUS LINE.  @H@@@@. IF SO, DO NOT PRINT THIS LINE, BUT INDICBT
)@@G@@ATE, VIA A '*' ON THE NEXT PRINTED  @C@@@@. LINE, THAT AT LEAST ONE LINEBU
)@@G@@ HAS BEEN SKIPPED.@[@@@@.     @D@@@@LINELOOP  LA        A0,R4           BV
)@@G@@  GET LINE NUMBER @F@@@@          JZ        A0,PRINTLINE      IF LAST LIBW
)@@G@@NE, DON'T SKIP IT @F@@@@          LR        R1,WPL            GET # OF WBX
)@@G@@ORDS PER LINE     @G@@@@          LA        A0,LASTWD         GET LAST WBY
)@@G@@ORD FROM PREVIOUS LINE  @H@@@@          LX        A1,X4             COPYBZ
)@@G@@ CURRENT INDEX AND INCREMENT TO A1  @G@@@@          SNE       A0,0,*A1  CA
)@@G@@        ANYTHING DIFFERENT ON THIS LINE?  @E@@@@          J         $+2 CB
)@@G@@              NO, SKIP THIS LINE    @E@@@@          J         PRINTLINE CC
)@@G@@        YES, PRINT THIS LINE  @E@@@@          LA,U      A6,1            CD
)@@G@@  SET SKIP INDICATOR    @E@@@@          AX        X4,WPL            POINCE
)@@G@@T TO NEXT LINE    @D@@@@          J         NEXTLINE          SKIP THIS CF
)@@G@@LINE  @[@@@@.     @E@@@@. WE DON'T WANT TO SKIP THIS LINE:  COMPOSE AND CG
)@@G@@PRINT IT    @[@@@@.     @C@@@@PRINTLINE E$DIT     EDPACK            OPENCH
)@@G@@ EDIT @F@@@@          LR        R2,A6             HOLD PREVIOUS SKIP INDCI
)@@G@@ICATOR@F@@@@          LA,U      A6,0              CLEAR NEW SKIP INDICATCJ
)@@G@@OR    @G@@@@          LA,U      A0,0,X4           GET INDEX OF FIRST WORCK
)@@G@@D IN LINE   @E@@@@          ANA       A0,BUFAD          MAKE IT RELATIVECL
)@@G@@ TO 0 @D@@@@          E$OCTF    4                 EDIT THE NUMBER @D@@@@CM
)@@G@@          E$SKIP    1                 SKIP A SPACE    @E@@@@          LACN
)@@G@@,U      A0,' '            ASSUME ANOTHER SPACE  @G@@@@          TZ      CO
)@@G@@  R2                BUT WAS SKIP FLAG PREVIOUSLY SET? @F@@@@          LACP
)@@G@@,U      A0,'*'            YES, INDICATE SKIPPED LINES @F@@@@          E$CQ
)@@G@@CHAR    .                 EDIT A SPACE OR ASTERISK    @F@@@@          LRCR
)@@G@@        R2,WPL            GET # OF WORDS PER LINE     @D@@@@          JGCS
)@@G@@D       R2,$+1            LESS 1 FOR JGD  @[@@@@.     @H@@@@. EDIT PROPECT
)@@G@@R NUMBER OF WORDS PER LINE.  THE LAST LINE MAY BE A PARTIAL LINE. @[@@@@CU
)@@G@@.     @G@@@@WORDLOOP  E$OCTF    12,0,*X4          EDIT VALUE AND POINT TCV
)@@G@@O NEXT WORD @E@@@@          E$SKIP    2                 2 SPACES BETWEENCW
)@@G@@ WORDS@E@@@@          LA,U      A0,0,X4           GET CURRENT WORD INDEXCX
)@@G@@@E@@@@          ANA       A0,BUFAD          MAKE IT RELATIVE TO 0 @D@@@@CY
)@@G@@          TLE       A0,NWRDS          ALL DONE YET?   @F@@@@.           CZ
)@@G@@                          IF SO, MAY BE PARTIAL LINE  @G@@@@          JGDA
)@@G@@D       R2,WORDLOOP       NO, GO BACK AND FINISH THIS LINE  @G@@@@      DB
)@@G@@    P$RINT    POUT              DONE WITH THIS LINE:  PRINT IT    @[@@@@DC
)@@G@@.     @H@@@@. SAVE LAST WORD OF THIS LINE FOR SKIP COMPARISON, AND SET FDD
)@@G@@OR NEXT LINE.     @[@@@@.     @E@@@@NEXTLINE  LA,U      A0,0,X4         DE
)@@G@@  GET CURRENT WORD INDEX@F@@@@          ANA,U     A0,1              BACKDF
)@@G@@ UP TO LAST WORD PRINTED@G@@@@          LA        A0,0,A0           PICKDG
)@@G@@ UP THE LAST WORD PRINTED     @F@@@@          SA        A0,LASTWD       DH
)@@G@@  AND STORE IT FOR SKIP TEST  @E@@@@          JGD       R4,LINELOOP     DI
)@@G@@  MORE LINES?  DO THEM  @F@@@@          J         0,X10             ALL DJ
)@@G@@DONE:  RETURN TO CALLER @ @@@@          OFF       SNAPSUB   @ @@@@      DK
)@@G@@    OFF       SNAPOK    @#@@@@          END     ___T TO A1  @G@@@@      DL

)@@G@@        YES, BETTER IGNORE TAPES    @ @@@@          OFF       OLDSTUFF  TK
)@@G@@@ @@@@          ON        BRKOK     @G@@@@          TNZ       BRKTSP    TL

)@@G@@K     @D@@@@          TNZ       BPT               IS B-OPTION SET?@C@@@@TN

)@@G@@BSORT         AUTOMATICALLY DONE BY B-OPT?@F@@@@          J         IN13TR
)@@G@@00            YES, JUST DO IT AT THE END  @[@@@@.     @ @@@@. CREATE SORTS
)@@G@@T KEY PARAMETER   @[@@@@.     @F@@@@IN1250    LA        A0,TB4ADS       TT
)@@G@@  GET ASSUMED SORT DIRECTION  @F@@@@          TNZ       SDTHSP          TU
)@@G@@  REVERSE SORT FOR THIS SPEC? @C@@@@          J         IN1252          TV
)@@G@@  NO, GO ON @F@@@@          TNE,U     A0,'D'            DESCENDING SORT TW
)@@G@@ASSUMED?    @E@@@@          LA,U      A0,'A'-('D'-'A')  YES, ADJUST VALUTX
)@@G@@E     @E@@@@          AA,U      A0,'D'-'A'        REVERSE SORT DIRECTIONTY
)@@G@@@F@@@@.                                     ('A' -> 'D' OR 'D' -> 'A')  TZ
)@@G@@@F@@@@IN1252    SA,S3     A0,TEMPKEY        STORE A/D SORT INDICATOR    UA

)@@G@@1,-1)         SET INDEX INTO J TABLE@D@@@@          SE,H1     A0,JTAB+1,UI

)@@G@@@F@@@@.                                     NOTE THAT 'BREAK' CODE BELOWUL
)@@G@@@F@@@@.                                     ASSUMES J-DES IS IN LOWER A3UM
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @F@@@@. MOST OF THE SPECS WITH ASSUMED VALUES HAVE SINGLE-BIUN
)@@G@@T VALUES AND@D@@@@. TESTS.  FOR THESE, WE WILL DO A SINGLE-BIT SORT.    UO
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @F@@@@          LA,U      A2,0              ASSUME NO ADJUSTUP
)@@G@@MENTS NEEDED@F@@@@          TNZ       TB4VAL            ASSUMED VALUE FOUQ

)@@G@@ALUE  @D@@@@          LSC       A1,A2             FIND FIRST BIT  @F@@@@UX
)@@G@@          AN,U      A2,29             COMPENSATE.  IF THE VALUE   @F@@@@UY
)@@G@@.                                     IS 2**5 (040), A2=0 BECAUSE @G@@@@UZ
)@@G@@.                                     THE MS BIT IS ALREADY CORRECT     VA
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @D@@@@. NOTE THAT TB4VAL IS ASSUMED TO BE A 6-BIT FIELD     VB
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @E@@@@          A         A0,A2             ADJUST THE MS BIVC
)@@G@@T     @E@@@@          LA,U      A2,1              FLAG SINGLE-BIT SORT  VD
)@@G@@@F@@@@IN1260    SA,S4     A0,TEMPKEY        STORE IN SORT KEY PARAMETER VE
)@@G@@@F@@@@.                                     WORD 1 OF PARAM COMPLETE    VF

)@@G@@J     @F@@@@          TZ        A2                BUT IS IT A SINGLE-BITVH

)@@G@@1     @E@@@@          JNZ       A3,IN1270         IF PARTIAL WORD, GO ONVJ

)@@G@@@ @@@@          ON        BRKOK     @F@@@@          LXI       A3,A2     VO
)@@G@@        SAVE WORD # FOR BREAK, BELOW@ @@@@          OFF       BRKOK     VP

)@@G@@    SA        A2,KEYIDX         RESET ADDKEYS INDEX   @ @@@@          ONVV

)@@G@@SP            BREAK THIS SPEC?@B@@@@          J         IN1290          VY

)@@G@@@E@@@@          TP        TB4BITS           SHOULD IT BE 'DL A0'  @B@@@@WA

)@@G@@              ASSUME 0 LEFT, 0 RIGHT SHIFT@E@@@@          TOP,U     A0,JWJ
)@@G@@SPECIAL       SPECIAL J-DESIGNATOR? @C@@@@          J         IN1278    WK

)@@G@@IGNIFICANT BIT (BIT 35 = 1)   @H@@@@          ANA,U     A0,1            WM

)@@G@@8             MOVE LEFT SHIFT COUNT TO UPPER A0 @F@@@@          LXM,U   WO
)@@G@@  A0,36             GET WORD LENGTH IN LOWER A0 @H@@@@          ANA     WP
)@@G@@  A0,JBITS,A3       CALCULATE RIGHT SHIFT COUNT (0 = NONE)  @G@@@@      WQ
)@@G@@    SA        A0,A4             SET LEFT,RIGHT SIFT COUNTS IN A4  @F@@@@WR
)@@G@@IN1278    LA        A3,( TE A0,2,*X5) GET A 'TE A0' INSTRUCTION   @F@@@@WS
)@@G@@          TP        TB4BITS           SHOULD IT BE A 'DTE A0'     @C@@@@WT

)@@G@@  A1,TB4VAL         GET ASSUMED VALUE IF ANY    @F@@@@          JZ      WV

)@@G@@  A0,TB4OP          YES, GET ASSUMED OPERATION  @C@@@@          TE,U    WX
)@@G@@  A0,TOP            IS IT TOP?@C@@@@          TNE,U     A0,TEP          WY
)@@G@@     OR TEP?@B@@@@          J         $+2               YES @D@@@@      WZ

)@@G@@  A3,( LMJ X11,BRKBIT)  GET AN 'LMJ X11,BRKBIT' INSTR @D@@@@IN1280    LAXB
)@@G@@        A0,BRKPNT         GET TABLE INDEX @E@@@@          NOP       0,0,XC

)@@G@@NT          . INCREMENT BREAK COUNT BY 1  @ @@@@          OFF       BRKOXO
)@@G@@K     @F@@@@IN1290    TZ        TB4VAL            SPEC WITH ASSUMED VALUXP
)@@G@@E?    @F@@@@          J         IN1080            YES, USER WANTS SORT OXQ
)@@G@@N IT, @F@@@@.                                     SO THAT'S ALL WE DO WIXR
)@@G@@TH IT @]@@@@IN1300    . @ @@@@          OFF       SORTOK    @F@@@@      XS
)@@G@@    TNZ       TB4VAL            ASSUMED VALUE FOR THIS ITEM?@C@@@@      XT
)@@G@@    J         IN1310            NO, GO ON @[@@@@.     @F@@@@. DON'T PERMXU
)@@G@@IT USER TO OVERRIDE OPERATION, J-DESIGNATOR, ETC., FOR@B@@@@. THE SPECIAXV
)@@G@@L ITEMS WITH ASSUMED VALUES.  @[@@@@.     @E@@@@          LA        A0,EXW
)@@G@@LT$           GET SPEC INDICATORS   @E@@@@          SSL       A0,6      XX
)@@G@@        MOVE (FCY)/RK/WK TO H2@G@@@@          TZ,U      0,A0            XY
)@@G@@  IF ANY OF THOSE ARE SPECIFIED,    @D@@@@          LMJ       X10,SPECERXZ
)@@G@@           SPEC ERROR   @D@@@@          TZ,S1     ELT$+1            VALUYA
)@@G@@E GIVEN?    @D@@@@          LMJ       X10,SPECER        YES, SPEC ERROR YB
)@@G@@@E@@@@          SR,S1     R15,ELT$+1        SET VALUE-GIVEN FLAG  @C@@@@YC
)@@G@@IN1310    TZ,S4     ELT$              OP GIVEN? @D@@@@          J       YD
)@@G@@  IN1330            YES, CONTINUE   @F@@@@          TZ        TB4OP     YE
)@@G@@        ASSUMED TEST FOR THIS ITEM? @E@@@@          TNZ,S1    ELT$+1    YF
)@@G@@        YES, WAS VALUE GIVEN? @F@@@@          J         IN1320          YG
)@@G@@  NO, HANDLE POSSIBLE ERROR   @[@@@@.     @F@@@@. NOTE THAT THE ABOVE TEYH
)@@G@@ST WILL NOT WORK PROPERLY IF THE ASSUMED  @B@@@@. TEST FOR AN ITEM IS TZYI
)@@G@@, TNZ, TP, OR TN. @[@@@@.     @E@@@@          LA        A2,TB4OP        YJ
)@@G@@  GET ASSUMED TEST INDEX@E@@@@          LA,H1     A0,OPCODE-1,A2    GET YK
)@@G@@PROPER OP CODE    @E@@@@          SA,H1     A0,ELT$+7         STORE AS IYL

)@@G@@IN1320    . @ @@@@          ON        SNAPOK    @E@@@@          TZ      YO

)@@G@@80            YES, NO VALUE   NO    @ @@@@          OFF       SNAPOK    YQ
)@@G@@@ @@@@          ON        SORTOK    @E@@@@          TZ        SRTHSP    YR

)@@G@@  YES, OK   @ @@@@          OFF       SORTOK    @G@@@@          LMJ     YT
)@@G@@  X10,SPECER        NO OPERATION, AND NOT SNAP OR SORT@[@@@@.     @D@@@@YU
)@@G@@. DETERMINE WHICH WORD OF DIRECTORY ITEM TO CHECK     @[@@@@.     @D@@@@YV
)@@G@@IN1330    LA        A0,TESTS          GET TEST COUNT  @H@@@@          MSYW
)@@G@@I,U     A0,SSIZE          ADJUST FOR SUPER SPEC TABLE ENTRY SIZE  @G@@@@YX

)@@G@@@F@@@@          LA        A0,INITLOAD       GET INITIAL LOAD INSTRUCTIONYZ

)@@G@@VALUE @E@@@@          LX,U      X10,IN1400        SET SUBROUTINE RETURN ZI
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @E@@@@. SUBROUTINE TO RETURN SORT RECORD WORD # IN A2, BASEDZJ
)@@G@@ ON   @A@@@@. SPECIFIED+ASSUMED ITEM OFFSET.    @[@@@@.     @A@@@@.     ZK
)@@G@@  ENTER VIA:  LMJ  X10,IN1340 @ @@@@.                   <RETURN>  @[@@@@ZL
)@@G@@.     @A@@@@.        DESTROYS:  A0, A2, X10     @[@@@@.     @E@@@@IN1340ZM
)@@G@@    LA,U      A2,0              INITIALIZE WORD #     @E@@@@          LAZN
)@@G@@,S3     A0,ELT$           FCYCLE CHAR COUNT     @E@@@@          JZ      ZO
)@@G@@  A0,IN1350         IF NONE, ASSUME WORD 0@^@@@@          TG,U      A0,3ZP
)@@G@@@D@@@@          LMJ       X10,SPECER        MAX 2 CHARS     @E@@@@      ZQ
)@@G@@    AA,S1     A2,ELT$+6         1ST CHAR OF FCYCLE    @D@@@@          ANZR
)@@G@@,U      A2,060            STRIP OFF FD    @C@@@@          TP        A2  ZS
)@@G@@              NEGATIVE? @E@@@@          LMJ       X10,SPECER        IF NZT
)@@G@@OT NUMBER, ERROR  @C@@@@          TNE,U     A0,1              1 CHAR?   ZU
)@@G@@@B@@@@          J         IN1350            YES @E@@@@          MSI,U   ZV
)@@G@@  A2,10             MOVE TO TENS PLACE    @D@@@@          AA,S2     A2,EZW
)@@G@@LT$+6         ADD UNITS DIGIT @D@@@@          ANA,U     A2,'0'          ZX
)@@G@@  STRIP OFF FD    @E@@@@IN1350    AA        A2,TB4WRD         ADD ASSUMEZY
)@@G@@D OFFSET    @D@@@@          LA        A0,TB4ITM         GET ITEM INDEX  ZZ
)@@G@@@G@@@@          MSI,U     A0,28             POINT TO PROPER ITEM IN RECOAA
)@@G@@RD    @ @@@@          AA        A2,A0     @E@@@@          J         0,X1AB
)@@G@@0             RETURN WORD # IN A2   @[@@@@.     @F@@@@IN1400    SA,H2   AC
)@@G@@  A2,SSLOAD,X6      STORE IN SUPER SPEC TABLE   @[@@@@.     @ @@@@. CHECAD
)@@G@@K FOR LEGAL OPERATION   @[@@@@.     @E@@@@          LA,H1     A0,ELT$+7 AE
)@@G@@        GET OPERATION (RKEY)  @D@@@@          LR,U      R1,OPCODL       AF
)@@G@@  # OF OPCODES    @E@@@@          LA        A3,(1,0)          FROM OPCODAG
)@@G@@E TABLE     @C@@@@          SE,H1     A0,OPCODE,*A3     FIND?     @C@@@@AH
)@@G@@          LMJ       X10,SPECER        NO, ERROR @G@@@@          LA,U    AI

)@@G@@,U      A10,DTE           DTE?@D@@@@          J         IN1440          AK
)@@G@@  NO, CONTINUE    @E@@@@          TZ,S5     ELT$              J-DESIGNATAL
)@@G@@OR GIVEN?   @F@@@@          LMJ       X10,SPECER        YES, CAN'T HAVE AM
)@@G@@J-DES ON DTE@E@@@@          TNZ,S1    ELT$+1            WAS A VALUE GIVEAN
)@@G@@N?    @E@@@@          LMJ       X10,SPECER        NO, MUST HAVE A VALUE AO
)@@G@@@F@@@@          LA        A0,INITDTE        GET INITIAL DTE INSTRUCTION AP
)@@G@@@G@@@@          AA        A0,X6             POINT TO PROPER SSPVAL TABLEAQ
)@@G@@ ADDR @F@@@@          SA        A0,SSTEST,X6      STORE IN SUPER SPEC TAAR
)@@G@@BLE   @F@@@@          LA,H1     A0,( DL A0,0,X8)  GET A 'DL A0,X,X8' INSAS
)@@G@@TR    @E@@@@          SA,H1     A0,SSLOAD,X6      CHANGE 'LA' TO 'DL'   AT
)@@G@@@C@@@@          J         IN1490            CONTINUE  @[@@@@.     @^@@@@AU
)@@G@@. OPERATION IS NOT DTE  @[@@@@.     @F@@@@IN1440    LA,S4     A0,OPCODE-AV
)@@G@@1,A3    GET OCTAL CODE FOR THIS OP  @G@@@@          SA,S1     A0,SSTEST,AW
)@@G@@X6      STORE IT IN REMOTE TEST INSTR     @[@@@@.     @B@@@@. CHECK FOR AX
)@@G@@LEGAL J-DESIGNATOR, IF GIVEN  @[@@@@.     @F@@@@          TZ,S5     ELT$AY
)@@G@@              J-DESIGNATOR (WKEY) PRESENT?@D@@@@          J         IN14AZ
)@@G@@70            YES, HANDLE IT  @G@@@@          LA        A0,TB4J         BA
)@@G@@  NO, GET ASSUMED J FOR THIS ITEM   @E@@@@          JZ        A0,IN1490 BB
)@@G@@        IF FULL WORD, SKIP IT @C@@@@          J         IN1480          BC
)@@G@@  CONTINUE  @F@@@@IN1470    LA,H1     A0,ELT$+8         PICK UP SPECIFIEBD
)@@G@@D J-DES     @D@@@@          LR,U      R1,JTABL          LENGTH OF TABLE BE
)@@G@@@E@@@@          LA        A1,(1,-1)         SEARCH J-DESIG TABLE  @C@@@@BF
)@@G@@          SE,H1     A0,JTAB+1,*A1     FIND?     @C@@@@          LMJ     BG
)@@G@@  X10,SPECER        NO, ERROR @E@@@@          LA,U      A0,,A1          BH
)@@G@@  A0 NOW CONTAINS J CODE@E@@@@IN1480    LA        A1,JFLAGS,A0      PCIKBI
)@@G@@ UP JDES FLAGS    @E@@@@          TEP,U     A1,JSPECIAL       SPECIAL J-BJ
)@@G@@DESIGNATOR? @F@@@@          J         IN1490            YES, DON'T MODIFBK
)@@G@@Y SSLOAD    @F@@@@          LSSL      A0,8              MOVE J CODE INTOBL
)@@G@@ POSITION   @F@@@@          OR,H1     A0,SSLOAD,X6      COMPOSITE LOAD IBM
)@@G@@NSTR IN A1  @G@@@@          SA,H1     A1,SSLOAD,X6      STORE BACK IN SUBN
)@@G@@PER SPEC TABLE    @D@@@@          SSL       A0,8              MOVE J BACBO
)@@G@@K     @[@@@@.     @ @@@@. OPCODE INDEX REMAINS IN A10 @[@@@@.     @G@@@@BP
)@@G@@. ASSUME SPECIFIED TEST VALUE IS FIELDATA, AND STORE IT.  IF NECESSARY, BQ
)@@G@@@F@@@@. SET SHIFT VALUE (SSHIFT) TO PERMIT SPECS LIKE  MI0(7)/TE/S1.C  .BR
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @G@@@@IN1490    DL        A2,ELT$+9         GET SUPER SPEC EBS
)@@G@@LEMENT (VALUE)    @E@@@@          TNZ,S1    ELT$+1            IF NO VALUBT
)@@G@@E WAS GIVEN,@E@@@@          DSL       A2,72                USE ZEROES INBU
)@@G@@STEAD @D@@@@          DS        A2,SSPVAL,X6      STORE SPEC VALUE@H@@@@BV
)@@G@@          TNE,U     A10,DTE           DOES THIS SPEC REQUIRE A DOUBLE TEBW
)@@G@@ST?   @F@@@@          J         IN1800            YES, ALL DONE WITH THIBX
)@@G@@S SPEC@H@@@@          LA        A1,JMSBIT,A0      GET MOST SIGNIFICANT BBY
)@@G@@IT (BIT 35 = 1)   @F@@@@          ANA,U     A1,1              ADJUST (0 BZ
)@@G@@IF NO LEFT SHIFT) @E@@@@          SA,H1     A1,SSHIFT,X6      STORE LEFTCA
)@@G@@ SHIFT COUNT@G@@@@.                                     VALUE IS ALREADYCB
)@@G@@ LEFT-JUSTIFIED,  @F@@@@.                                        SO DON'CC
)@@G@@T SHIFT IT NOW    @D@@@@          LA,U      A1,36             GET WORD LCD
)@@G@@ENGTH @G@@@@          ANA       A1,JBITS,A0       COMPUTE RIGHT SHIFT (0CE
)@@G@@ IF NONE)   @F@@@@          SA,H2     A1,SSHIFT,X6      STORE RIGHT SHIFCF
)@@G@@T COUNT     @F@@@@          LA        A3,JFLAGS,A0      PICK UP J-DESIGNCG
)@@G@@ATOR FLAGS  @E@@@@          TEP,U     A3,JSIGN          SIGN-EXTENDED J CH
)@@G@@FIELD?@F@@@@          J         IN1492            YES, DO ALGEBRAIC SHIFCI
)@@G@@T     @G@@@@          SSL       A2,0,A1           NO, SHIFT VALUE RIGHT CJ
)@@G@@LOGICALLY   @C@@@@          J         IN1494            CONTINUE  @G@@@@CK
)@@G@@IN1492    SSA       A2,0,A1           SHIFT VALUE RIGHT ALGEBRAICLY     CL
)@@G@@@E@@@@IN1494    SA        A2,SSPVAL,X6      STORE SHIFTED VALUE   @E@@@@CM
)@@G@@          TOP,U     A3,JSPECIAL       SPECIAL J-DESIGNATOR? @E@@@@      CN
)@@G@@    SZ        SSHIFT,X6         NO, ZERO SHIFT COUNTS @[@@@@.     @G@@@@CO
)@@G@@. CHECK FOR MASK BEING SPECIFIED.  IF SO, SET MASK IN SUPER SPEC TABLE  CP
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @D@@@@          LA        A0,INITMASK       GET INITIAL MASKCQ
)@@G@@@E@@@@          SA        A0,SSMASK,X6      STORE IN SSMASK FIELD @E@@@@CR
)@@G@@          LA,S2     A3,ELT$+1         GET VERSION CHAR COUNT@E@@@@      CS
)@@G@@    JZ        A3,IN1600         IF NONE, ASSUME -0    @D@@@@          ANCT
)@@G@@,U      A3,1              LESS 1 FOR JGD  @G@@@@          LA,H1     A0,ECU
)@@G@@LT$+11        GET FIRST THREE CHARS OF VERSION  @C@@@@          TNE,U   CV
